# Batch 9 Status Ledger

Purpose: operational control for Batch 9 execution. This file prevents hidden progress, repeated work, and component drift.

Rule: before any Batch 9 code change, review and update the relevant row. After any interruption or final response, update `Status`, `Last blocker`, and `Next action`.

Status values:

- `Aprovado`: component passed contract, isolated story, reusable architecture, variants/states, real behavior, screenshot comparison, 1:1 visual review, and required validation gates.
- `Em ajuste`: implementation/certification started but a known blocker remains.
- `Implementado sem certificacao`: component exists but lacks final source-crop screenshot comparison and approval matrix.
- `Nao iniciado`: no certified component work has started for the current contract.

Broad gates:

- Batch 9 is complete only when every row is `Aprovado`.
- Batch 11 can start only after Batch 9 is closed, because image coverage must use already-approved components.
- Focused iteration may run package tests/typecheck first; full `test`, `lint`, `build`, and `visual:smoke` are required for component approval, component-family approval, or batch closure.
- Current execution focus, updated 2026-07-09: certify structural page families one by one at 99%/1:1 visual parity. A family is not approved from architecture alone; the family must use official reusable components/tokens and pass source-image visual comparison for every page in that structural family before moving to the next family.
